***свезти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свезти.html>свезти́</a> (15351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свезти.html>свезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свозить.html>свози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transport, to drive, to convey</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transport there and back, to drive there and back</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transport down, to drive down</li>
<li>to transport away, to carry away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to gather together</li></ol>

***свекла.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свекла</a> (11289)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from misreading <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свёкла</a></i> written without the trema since the times of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ликбез.html>ликбе́з</a></i> in the twentieth century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свекла́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sveklá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекла.html>свеклы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекла.html>свеклы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекла.html>свеко́л</a></b>)
</p>

***свекровь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свекровь.html>свекро́вь</a> (15674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">свекрꙑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svekry</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svekry</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекровь.html>свекро́вь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svekróvʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекровь.html>свекро́ви</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекровь.html>свекро́ви</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свекровь.html>свекро́вей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a woman’s mother-in-law <i>(husband’s mother only)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">свекру́ха</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svekrúxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial, can be disrespectful; or regional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свергающий.html>сверга́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svergájuščij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверкание.html>сверка́ние</a> (23439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sverkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкание.html>сверка́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverkánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкание.html>сверка́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкание.html>сверка́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкание.html>сверка́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glitter, sparkle, scintillation, glisten, glister</li>
<li>flash, flashing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">burst of light</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>glint</li>
<li>flare</li>
<li>glance</li>
<li>twinkle</li>
<li>coruscation</li>
<li>lambency</li></ol>

***сверкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ть</a> (3555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкнуть.html>сверкну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sparkle, to twinkle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пяток.html>пятками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sverkátʹ pjatkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take to one's heels</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to glitter</li>
<li>to glare
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молния.html>мо́лния</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mólnija <b>sverkájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">lightning is flashing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сверкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверкнуть.html>сверкну́ть</a> (5952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкнуть.html>сверкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>сверло́</a> (19419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*svьrdьlo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>сверло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sverló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>сверла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>свёрла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>свёрл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>drill, drill bit, auger, bore <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">carpenter's tool</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***свернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a> (2253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свертывать.html>свёртывать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сворачивать.html>свора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to displace, to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On s trudóm <b>svernúl</b> kámenʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>displaced</b> the stone with difficulty.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll up the carpet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:папироса.html>папиро́су</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> papirósu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll a cigarette</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> parusá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to furl sails</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to curtail, to reduce, to cut down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> proizvódstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to curtail production</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wind up, to bring to a close</li>
<li>to coagulate</li>
<li>to turn, to make a turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:направо.html>напра́во</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:налево.html>нале́во</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> naprávo (nalévo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn to the right (left)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹ</b> s dorógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn off the road</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to strip <i>(a screw, thread)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:свернуться.html>сверну́ться</a> (9637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуться.html>сверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">свёртываться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">свора́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to curl up, to roll up, to coil up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуться.html>сверну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клубок.html>клубко́м</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:клубочек.html>клубо́чком</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>svernútʹsja</b> klubkóm/klubóčkom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll oneself up into a ball</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lessen, to contract</li>
<li><i>(milk, cream)</i> to turn, to curdle, <i>(blood)</i> to coagulate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оставлять.html>оставля́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оно.html>оно́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуться.html>свернётся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne ostavljáj molokó na sólnce, a to onó <b>svernjótsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't leave the milk out in the sun or it will turn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свернуть.html>сверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверстник.html>све́рстник</a> (8489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съвьрстьникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭvĭrstĭnikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съвьрстьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭvĭrstĭnŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of the same age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съвьрсть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭvĭrstĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of the same age; coeval, age-mate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вьрста</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vĭrsta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">vȓst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">row, type, age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> (genitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">vrstȋ</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">वृत्ति</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vṛttí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">method, essence, nature, gender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Morphologically <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верста.html>верста́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">verstá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверстник.html>све́рстник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">svérstnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверстник.html>све́рстника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверстник.html>све́рстники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверстник.html>све́рстников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">све́рстница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contemporary</li>
<li>coeval</li>
<li>age-mate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who is the same age as another</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
